## Idea

We construct canonical pullbacks of cospans

## Properties

### Identity types can be presented as pullbacks

<pre class="Agda"><a id="cone-Id"></a><a id="2678" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#2678" class="Function">cone-Id</a> <a id="2686" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="2690" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2691" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#2691" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="2693" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2695" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="2700" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2702" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2703" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#2703" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2705" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2707" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2710" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#2691" class="Bound">l</a><a id="2711" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2713" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2714" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#2714" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2716" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#2716" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="2718" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2720" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#2703" class="Bound">A</a><a id="2721" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2723" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="2727" href="foundation-core.cones-pullbacks.html#1315" class="Function">cone</a> <a id="2732" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2733" href="foundation-core.constant-maps.html#216" class="Function">const</a> <a id="2739" href="foundation.unit-type.html#1084" class="Datatype">unit</a> <a id="2744" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#2703" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2746" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#2714" class="Bound">x</a><a id="2747" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2749" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2750" href="foundation-core.constant-maps.html#216" class="Function">const</a> <a id="2756" href="foundation.unit-type.html#1084" class="Datatype">unit</a> <a id="2761" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#2703" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2763" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#2716" class="Bound">y</a><a id="2764" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2766" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2767" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#2714" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2769" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="2771" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#2716" class="Bound">y</a><a id="2772" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="3758" class="Comment">{- One way to solve this exercise is to show that Id (pr1 t) (pr2 t) is a
   pullback for every t : A × A. This allows one to use path induction to
   show that the inverse of the gap map is a section.
-}</a>

### Dependent products of pullbacks are pullbacks
